A realistic canoo car interior with a white and black color scheme, showcasing an industrial style, perfectly proportioned and highly detailed. The photograph, taken by Annie Leibovitz using a Canon EOS R3 camera with professional studio lighting equipment including 3-point lighting, softbox flash, and various lighting techniques such as Half rear Lighting, Backlight, Natural Lighting, Incandescent, Optical Fiber, Moody Lighting, Cinematic Lighting, Studio Lighting, Soft Lighting, and Contre-Jour, captures the elegant beauty of the car interior in stunning quality. The image features intricate shadows, shimmering details, and realistic reflections achieved through advanced rendering techniques like Global Illumination, Screen Space Global Illumination, Ray Tracing Global Illumination, Ray Tracing Reflections, Lumen Reflections, Screen Space Reflections, and Ray Tracing Ambient Occlusion. The scene is further enhanced with post-processing effects such as Diffraction Grading, Chromatic Aberration, GB Displacement, Scan Lines, and other shader effects like OpenGL-Shaders and GLSL-Shaders, resulting in a visually captivating composition. This masterpiece of photography, with its ultra-high resolution of 46k, showcases the power of Unreal Engine 5 and the use of HDR and high contrast to create a moody and atmospheric ambiance.

A low angle shot of a Dodge Hellcat with a Liberty Walk bodykit in a photography studio, set against the mesmerizing Tokyo, Japan city skyline. The hyper realistic image showcases intricate details and cinematic lighting, creating a dark and moody atmosphere. The photo realistic rendering, captured with a high shutter speed of 1/1000 and a narrow aperture of F/22, delivers stunning depth of field and rich colors. The dog is wearing a stylish vogue and Adidas outfit, with a smooth and sharp focus making for a highly photorealistic and detailed shot, featuring depth of field effects to highlight the symmetrical eyes and terracotta color scheme. The shot is a full body middle shot portrait, taken on a Canon DSLR with an f/2.8 long exposure and 25mm lens.
